\wd witch
\thes witch
\is II.B.6.a
\nt The English terms 'witch', 'witchcraft' are used in Ghana English and some anthropological studies to refer to
people who harm others by non-material means, whether voluntarily or involuntarily, according to a complex of
beliefs which is similar in general but different in detail in each ethnic group.
\td 07/Apr/2016

\wd witchcraft
\thes witchcraft
\is II.B.6.a
\nt The English terms 'witch', 'witchcraft' are used in Ghana English
and some anthropological studies to refer to people who harm
others by non-material means, whether voluntarily or involuntarily,
according to a complex of beliefs which is similar in general but
different in detail in each ethnic group.

\wd %%
\nt NOTES on the THESAURUS
\nt 1. The entries aim to refer to concepts, not the vocabulary of any particular language.
\nt 2. The English keywords aim to characterise the concept and to be something an Engish-speaker might look up to find this concept.
\nt 3. The main purpose is that when the list is alphabetised on the index of semantics field (\is) the items will be grouped together in
semantically-related sets.
\nt 4. The ultimate aim is that the keywords and groupings will reveal and be adjusted to conform to the sememics of the Ghanaian languages.
\nt Tony Naden:
\td 06/Jun/2014
